Statistics

Problem Statement for "IncreasingSequences"

Problem Statement

You are given two int[]s L and R, each of length n.

Find the number of strictly increasing sequences of integers A[0] &lt; A[1] &lt; ... &lt; A[n-1] such that L[i] &le; A[i] &le; R[i] for every i. Return this number modulo 998244353.

Definition

Class:
IncreasingSequences
Method:
count
Parameters:
int[], int[]
Returns:
int
Method signature:
int count(int[] L, int[] R)
(be sure your method is public)

Constraints

  • n will be between 1 and 300, inclusive.
  • L will contain exactly n elements.
  • R will contain exactly n elements.
  • L[i] will be between 1 and 109, inclusive.
  • R[i] will be between L[i] and 109, inclusive.

Examples

  1. {1, 3, 1, 4}

    {6, 5, 4, 6}

    Returns: 4

    There are 4 strictly increasing sequences satisfying the conditions: {1, 3, 4, 5}, {1, 3, 4, 6}, {2, 3, 4, 5} and {2, 3, 4, 6}.

  2. {10, 30}

    {20, 40}

    Returns: 121

  3. {30, 10}

    {40, 20}

    Returns: 0

  4. {4, 46, 46, 35, 20, 77, 20}

    {41, 65, 84, 90, 49, 86, 88}

    Returns: 2470

  5. {1}

    {1000000000}

    Returns: 1755647

    Don't forget about the modulo.

  6. {1}

    {1}

    Returns: 1

  7. {1000000000}

    {1000000000}

    Returns: 1

  8. {1}

    {998244352}

    Returns: 998244352

  9. {1}

    {998244353}

    Returns: 0

  10. {1}

    {998244354}

    Returns: 1
